i just checked curriculum for IIT Ropar Mnc and compared it with IIT Mandi Mnc and found a few interesting points:

1. Mandi has a lot more free electives credits than ropar in the course which you can choose according to your liking.

Consider these points before making any choice if academics and placements matter to you.

Strong in pharma core (good for MS/PhD or jobs like DRDO, pharma companies).


Cons:

Limited core jobs unless you aim for pharma R&D or higher studies.

Heavy chemistry/chemical engineering baseâ€”can be dry if you're not interested.


Best for: Students open to either core pharma or using IIT BHUâ€™s reputation to pivot (coding, MBA, UPSC, etc.).



---

ğŸ—ï¸ 3. IIT Patna â€“ Civil Engineering

Pros:

Core jobs in PSUs, infrastructure firms.

IIT Patna has decent placement growth, though not elite yet.

Civil is relatively stable and known in India.


Cons:

Less flexibility in shifting to coding unless you put in extra effort.

Core civil jobs may have lower pay unless itâ€™s PSU.


Best for: Someone okay with core engineering or PSU goal, or ready to work hard to switch fields.



---

âœ… Priority Order Based on General Flexibility + Career Scope (and if you are not into core)

> 1. IIT Mandi Bio (more flexible; better coding and research options)
2. IIT BHU Pharma (older IIT, good brand, can switch with effort)
3. IIT Patna Civil (least flexible unless you're PSU/core-focused)




---

ğŸ§  Final Advice:

If you're interested in tech/coding, prefer Mandi Bio (more flexibility and better environment for coding).

If you want brand + options for MBA/Govt/PhD, BHU Pharma is solid.

If you're okay with Civil/PSU or will do coding on the side rigorously, Patna Civil is fine.


Let me know your interests (coding, core, UPSC, abroad, etc.), and I can personalize it more!
